+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        a_base = wave_m * 256 + lane * 4
+        b_base = wave_n * 256 + lane * 4
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag_words[i] = a_words[a_base + i]
+            b_frag_words[i] = b_words[b_base + i]
+        m_a = S.view(a_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        a_base = wave_m * 256 + lane * 4
+        b_base = wave_n * 256 + lane * 4
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag_words[i] = a_words[a_base + i]
+            b_frag_words[i] = b_words[b_base + i]
+        m_a = S.view(a_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.rsqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

class dtype:
    SINT_TYPES = ["i8", "i16", "i32", "i64"]
    UINT_TYPES = ["u1", "u8", "u16", "u32", "u64"]
    FP_TYPES = ["fp16", "bf16", "fp32", "fp64"]
    STANDARD_FP_TYPES = ["fp16", "bf16", "fp32", "fp64"]
    OTHER_TYPES = ["void"]

    def __init__(self, name):
        self.name = name
        assert name in dtype.SINT_TYPES + dtype.UINT_TYPES + dtype.FP_TYPES + dtype.OTHER_TYPES, name


# scalar types
# Signed integer types
i8 = dtype("i8")
i16 = dtype("i16")
i32 = dtype("i32")
i64 = dtype("i64")

# Unsigned integer types
u1 = dtype("u1")
u8 = dtype("u8")
u16 = dtype("u16")
u32 = dtype("u32")
u64 = dtype("u64")

# Floating-point types
f16 = dtype("fp16")
bf16 = dtype("bf16")
f32 = dtype("fp32")
f64 = dtype("fp64")

# Other types
void = dtype("void")


dynamic = -1


class Tensor:
    """Multi-dimensional tensor type."""

    def __init__(self, shape, element_ty):
        self.shape = shape
        self.element_ty = element_ty


class pointer_type:
    def __init__(self, element_ty):
        self.element_ty = element_ty


Pointer = pointer_type


class constexpr_type:
    def __init__(self, value):
        self.value = value

    def __eq__(self, other):
        return isinstance(other, constexpr_type) and self.value == other.value

    def __repr__(self) -> str:
        return f"constexpr_type[{self.value}]"


class constexpr:
    """
    This class is used to store a value that is known at compile-time.
    """

    def __init__(self, value):
        while isinstance(value, constexpr):
            value = value.value
        self.value = value
        self.type = constexpr_type(value)

    def __repr__(self) -> str:
        return f"constexpr[{self.value}]"

    def __hash__(self):
        return hash((self.value, self.type))

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(

+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N

+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M

+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32

+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)

+        m_b = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

+

+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        a_base = wave_m * 256 + lane * 4
+        b_base = wave_n * 256 + lane * 4
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag_words[i] = a_words[a_base + i]
+            b_frag_words[i] = b_words[b_base + i]
+        m_a = S.view(a_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)
+
+
 @substrate.jit

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.rsqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_frag_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        a_base = wave_m * 256 + lane * 4
+        b_base = wave_n * 256 + lane * 4
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            a_frag_words[i] = a_words[a_base + i]
+            b_frag_words[i] = b_words[b_base + i]
+        m_a = S.view(a_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_frag_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.rsqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

codex
I found a more promising route that stays within the examples Substrate already exercises: typed `view` on a shared-memory subview, then index the lane row exactly like the standalone MFMA example. That should avoid the problematic ad hoc register assembly.

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.rsqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.rsqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2

+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

The kernel is running but numerically off, which means the remaining bug is in the MFMA data mapping or writeback. I’m isolating the GEMM stage directly against a torch reference so I can correct the specific swizzle/writeback mistake instead of guessing.

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2

+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(

+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5

+            lane1 = lane0 + 1

+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE

+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

    v=float(cur[r,c])

    idx_base=row_quad*8

+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(

+            )

+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]

+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1

+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(

+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

codex
I have a cleaner way to recover the writeback layout than noisy random matching: I’m using a synthetic GEMM where every logical `(row, col)` in the first tile encodes itself as `col + row/32`. That lets me decode the true destination of each accumulator value directly from the output.
exec
/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch, math
path='/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p62/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('mod', path)
mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec); spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

x=torch.zeros((mod.BATCH_SIZE, mod.INPUT_SIZE), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
w=torch.zeros((mod.HIDDEN_SIZE, mod.INPUT_SIZE), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
b=torch.zeros((mod.HIDDEN_SIZE,), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
for r in range(64):
    x[r,0]=1
    x[r,1]=torch.tensor(r/32, dtype=torch.float32).to(torch.bfloat16)
for c in range(64):
    w[c,0]=torch.tensor(float(c), dtype=torch.float32).to(torch.bfloat16)
    w[c,1]=1

tmp=torch.empty((mod.BATCH_SIZE, mod.HIDDEN_SIZE), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
mod.gemm_bias_mfma_kernel[mod._launch_gemm](x, w, b, tmp)
cur=tmp[:32,:32].float().cpu()
for lane in range(8):
    out=[]
    lane_row=lane & 15
    lane_col_group=lane >> 4
    for row_quad in range(2):
        row=lane_row + row_quad*16
        idx_base=row_quad*8
        for j in range(4):
            col=lane_col_group*4+j
            v=float(cur[row,col])
            tc=math.floor(v+1e-3)
            tr=int(round((v-tc)*32))
            out.append(((row,col),v,(tr,tc)))
        for j in range(4):
            col=lane_col_group*4+16+j
            v=float(cur[row,col])
            tc=math.floor(v+1e-3)
            tr=int(round((v-tc)*32))
            out.append(((row,col),v,(tr,tc)))

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            a_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane0 = row_in_wave * 2
+            lane1 = lane0 + 1
+            base0 = wave_sel * 256 + lane0 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            base1 = wave_sel * 256 + lane1 * 4 + load_part * 2
+            b_words[base0 + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base0 + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base1 + 0] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base1 + 1] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
