+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v

+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]

+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))

+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]

+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)

The current LDS packing was too aggressive. The prompt’s swizzle note points to a simpler, lane-stable layout: each 16-byte chunk should stay intact per lane, with the two natural halves consumed directly by the two MFMA steps. I’m switching the A/B packing to that contiguous-per-lane form now.

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):

+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)

+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)
+
+
 @substrate.jit
-def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((INPUT_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16), GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16), GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16)):

-        for j in S.range(HIDDEN_SIZE):

-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t

-            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)

-                var += d * d
-            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
-            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
-                c = g * GROUP_SIZE + t
-                v = (S.convert(Y[i, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-                v = v * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[c], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[c], S.f32)
-                if v < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(

+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):

+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+

+
+    S.syncthreads()
+

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
+

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 19] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 7] + bias3, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+

+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2

+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))

+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    bias0 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0], S.f32)
+    bias1 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1], S.f32)
+    bias2 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2], S.f32)
+    bias3 = S.convert(BIAS0[warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row = warp_row + lane_row + row_quad * 16
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 0] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 0] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 1] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 1] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 2] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 2] + bias2, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 3] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 3] + bias3, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 16] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4] + bias0, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 17] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 5] + bias1, S.bf16)
+        TMP[row, warp_col + lane_col_group * 4 + 18] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 6] + bias2, S.bf16)

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),

+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+

+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)

The synthetic tile decode pinned down the accumulator writeback pattern. The MFMA result is column-oriented per lane, not row-oriented, and the bias needs to follow that same column ownership. I’m correcting the store mapping now.

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    out_col = warp_col + lane_row + (lane_col_group & 1) * 16
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row_base = warp_row + row_quad * 16 + (lane_col_group >> 1) * 4
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            TMP[row_base + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+            TMP[row_base + 8 + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4 + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+
+

     def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, num_groups, eps=1e-05, negative_slope=0.01):

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    out_col = warp_col + lane_row + (lane_col_group & 1) * 16
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row_base = warp_row + row_quad * 16 + (lane_col_group >> 1) * 4
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            TMP[row_base + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+            TMP[row_base + 8 + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4 + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+
+
+class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, num_groups, eps=1e-05, negative_slope=0.01):
         super().__init__()
         self.fc = nn.Linear(input_size, hidden_size)

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    out_col = warp_col + lane_row + (lane_col_group & 1) * 16
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row_base = warp_row + row_quad * 16 + (lane_col_group >> 1) * 4
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            TMP[row_base + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+            TMP[row_base + 8 + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4 + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+
+

+def gemm_bias_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    W_T: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WAVE_SIZE
+    wave = tid // WAVE_SIZE
+    wave_m = wave // WAVES_N
+    wave_n = wave % WAVES_N
+
+    block_m = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_n = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row = block_m + wave_m * 32
+    warp_col = block_n + wave_n * 32
 
-class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    a_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_M * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((WAVES_N * 64 * 4,), S.u32)
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, X_RANGE_BYTES)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W_T, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // BLOCK_K):
+        k_base = k0 * BLOCK_K
+
+        if tid < 128:
+            load_row = tid >> 1
+            load_part = tid & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_m + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                x_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            a_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            a_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            a_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            a_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+        else:
+            t = tid - 128
+            load_row = t >> 1
+            load_part = t & 1
+            row_bytes = ((block_n + load_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k_base + load_part * 8) * 2
+            vec = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                w_rsrc, zero, S.convert(row_bytes, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            wave_sel = load_row >> 5
+            row_in_wave = load_row & 31
+            lane_swz = row_in_wave + load_part * 32
+            base = wave_sel * 256 + lane_swz * 4
+            b_words[base + 0] = vec[0]
+            b_words[base + 1] = vec[1]
+            b_words[base + 2] = vec[2]
+            b_words[base + 3] = vec[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        pack_layout = S.make_layout((64, 4), (4, 1))
+        a_wave_words = S.subview(a_words, (wave_m * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        b_wave_words = S.subview(b_words, (wave_n * 256,), (256,), (1,))
+        a_packed = S.view(a_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        b_packed = S.view(b_wave_words, S.u32, pack_layout)
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_row = lane & 15
+    lane_col_group = lane >> 4
+    out_col = warp_col + lane_row + (lane_col_group & 1) * 16
+    bias = S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)
+
+    for row_quad in S.range(2):
+        row_base = warp_row + row_quad * 16 + (lane_col_group >> 1) * 4
+        idx_base = row_quad * 8
+        for i in S.range(4):
+            TMP[row_base + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+            TMP[row_base + 8 + i, out_col] = S.convert(c_lane[idx_base + 4 + i] + bias, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def groupnorm_leakyrelu_mul2_kernel(
+    TMP: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+    GN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    GN_BIAS: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, HIDDEN_SIZE), S.bf16),
+):
+    row = S.block_id(0)
+    group = S.block_id(1)
+    lane = S.thread_id(0)
+    channel = group * GROUP_SIZE + lane
+
+    shared_vals = S.make_shared((GROUP_SIZE,), S.f32)
+    v = S.convert(TMP[row, channel], S.f32)
+    shared_vals[lane] = v
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    if lane == 0:
+        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            mean += shared_vals[i]
+        mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+        for i in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
+            d = shared_vals[i] - mean
+            var += d * d
+        var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
+
+        shared_vals[0] = mean
+        shared_vals[1] = S.convert(1.0, S.f32) / S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
+
+    S.syncthreads()
+
+    mean = shared_vals[0]
+    inv_std = shared_vals[1]
+    out = (v - mean) * inv_std
+    out = out * S.convert(GN_WEIGHT[channel], S.f32) + S.convert(GN_BIAS[channel], S.f32)
+    if out < S.convert(0.0, S.f32):
+        out = out * S.convert(NEGATIVE_SLOPE, S.f32)
+    Y[row, channel] = S.convert(out + out, S.bf16)
+
+

     def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size, num_groups, eps=1e-05, negative_slope=0.01):

         self.fc = nn.Linear(input_size, hidden_size)

Implemented the optimized kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p62/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/output_model_new.py).

It now uses a 4-wave AMDGPU MFMA GEMM path with `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32`, vectorized `raw_buffer_load_x4`, LDS staging for A/B, and a separate substrate post kernel for group norm + leaky ReLU + multiply-by-2. `candidate_input.py` was not modified.

Validation passed with the required harness command. The latest round-local result in [debug_eval.jsonl](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p62/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/debug_eval.jsonl) shows `correctness: true` and candidate `runtime_us: 7.68`.

 NEGATIVE_SLOPE = 0.01
 EPS = 1e-05
 
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WAVE_SIZE = 64
+WAVES_M = 2
+WAVES_N = 2
+WAVES_PER_BLOCK = WAVES_M * WAVES_N
+THREADS_PER_BLOCK = WAVE_SIZE * WAVES_PER_BLOCK
+
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((HIDDEN_SIZE // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS_PER_BLOCK, 1, 1))
+

+def _launch_post():
+    return ((BATCH_SIZE, NUM_GROUPS, 1), (GROUP_SIZE, 1, 1))
